### 1. Liminal Transit Aesthetic Portrait

**Author**: [Human AI Gallery | Prompt Architect](https://x.com/HumanAIGallery)  **Date**: 2026-02-12  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化提示，用于生成具有“阈限过渡”美学的超广角（0.5 倍）肖像。画面中，一位 21 岁的潮流引领者坐在空荡荡的地铁站冰冷的地板上，强调刺眼的荧光灯、桶形畸变，以及冰冷、叛逆、原始的智能手机随拍风格。

![Liminal Transit Aesthetic Portrait](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964568753_ttfcx6_HA7iUd0XoAACq9X.jpg)

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "meta": {
      "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
      "style": "0.5x ultra-wide angle, liminal transit aesthetic"
    },
    "subject": {
      "description": "21-year-old trendsetter with a bored but magnetic presence",
      "face": "Looking down into the lens from a high angle (0.5x look), neutral model-esque expression, heavy dark eyeliner",
      "skin": "Pale and luminous under the station's fluorescent tubes, high contrast highlights",
      "hair": "Sleek back-combed 'wet look' or messy space buns",
      "pose": "Sitting on the cold floor of an empty subway station, legs extended towards the camera (distorted size), one hand on the floor for balance",
      "outfit": "Short pleated skirt, white button-down shirt (half-unbuttoned), oversized tie, knee-high leather boots with silver buckles"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Empty, modern subway station with white tiles",
      "background_elements": [
        "Infinite perspective of station pillars",
        "Blurred light trails of a passing train",
        "Yellow safety lines on the platform reflecting the overhead lights"
      ]
    },
    "lighting": {
      "type": "Clinical overhead fluorescent + Blue-ish ambient",
      "characteristics": [
        "Cold, desaturated color palette",
        "Harsh shadows beneath the eyes and jawline",
        "Long reflections on the polished floor"
      ]
    },
    "photography_style": {
      "style": "0.5x ultra-wide smartphone dump",
      "camera_look": "Barrel distortion at the frame edges, sharp digital texture",
      "imperfections": "Dust particles in the air, slight chromatic aberration, raw and unpolished feel",
      "mood": "Cold, rebellious, aesthetic, urban"
    }
  }
}
```

```

The background features a close-up of the aged wood of the house structure, covered in patches of green moss. The scene is illuminated by soft, diffused light typical of a rainy day. ![松林中的波西米亚风情编辑肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964565963_j87s4n_HA67ND_bIAAADXN.jpg)

```
Young woman with extremely long, sleek straight blonde hair cascading like liquid silk down her back, individual strands catching the light with soft golden highlights, captured in a graceful side-profile pose that emphasizes her delicate features and natural jawline. She wears a gentle, effortless smile — subtle, warm, and serene — eyes softly focused ahead as if lost in a peaceful moment within nature. Her posture is relaxed yet elegant, shoulders slightly turned, creating a refined feminine silhouette.

She stands surrounded by a dense forest of towering pine trees, their tall vertical trunks forming a majestic natural cathedral around her. The forest floor is textured with pine needles, soft moss, and scattered cones, adding rich earthy detail. Light filters down through high branches in soft golden rays, creating dreamy beams and dappled highlights across her hair, skin, and outfit. The atmosphere feels fresh and quiet, with a slight mist in the distance adding depth and cinematic layering.

She wears a handcrafted bohemian crochet top featuring intricate geometric patterns in warm beige, muted brown, and soft ivory white tones. The knit texture is highly detailed, showcasing delicate stitching, openwork designs, and artisanal craftsmanship. The off-shoulder neckline gently reveals her collarbones and upper shoulders, enhancing the romantic boho aesthetic. Dramatic bell sleeves flow loosely from her arms, adorned with airy cutout holes that allow glimpses of skin and create beautiful shadow patterns in the sunlight.

Her brown layered tulle skirt falls gracefully from the waist, featuring multiple soft translucent layers that create dimension and gentle movement. The fabric appears light and airy, slightly lifted by a soft forest breeze, adding a sense of motion and natural elegance. Around her neck rests a subtle layered necklace — fine chains with small organic pendants — complementing the earthy color palette. Her makeup is minimal and natural, glowing skin with soft blush tones, neutral lips, and lightly defined lashes to maintain a fresh outdoor look.

Photorealistic detail shot, ultra-high resolution 8K quality, sharp focus on subject with shallow depth of field softly blurring the pine forest background. Natural forest lighting, golden hour glow, cinematic composition, high dynamic range, realistic skin texture, visible fabric fibers, crisp hair strands, professional fashion photography style, dreamy boho editorial aesthetic, warm earthy color grading, atmospheric, ethereal, serene mood --ar 2:3 --stylize 250 --v 6
```

命中の瞬間はスローモーション。
強い衝撃波エフェクト、光の軌跡、ダイナミックなモーションブラー。

・高速ドリーインで少女に迫る
・ゾンビ接近時に手持ち風の激しい揺れ

### 19. 复古与现代风格姓名海报提示词

The scene begins completely still.

– The fog escapes naturally from inside the glass.
– Fog spills downward and outward in slow, fluid motion.
– The fog spreads into the surrounding space, filling the frame softly.
– The perfume bottle remains perfectly still on the pedestal.

Fog disperses realistically due to gravity and air flow.
No explosions.
No sudden bursts.
No fast motion.
Smooth cinematic diffusion only.

LIGHTING:

Luxury

### 43. Lavart Agent Jugemu 提示文本修正

**Author**: [ミサキ](https://x.com/misakin883)  **Date**: 2026-02-11  **Language**: ja

> 这条推文展示了 Lavart 代理在将其输入 Nano Banana Pro 之前，根据之前推文中复杂的文本螺旋提示（寿限无故事）生成的已更正日文文本。这展示了该代理的预处理能力。

![Lavart Agent Jugemu 提示文本修正](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770878362770_5v6b2q_HA3gTQ1asAA42UY.jpg)
![Lavart Agent Jugemu 提示文本修正](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770878362748_bgumpp_HA3gT8ta8AAJipw.jpg)
![Lavart Agent Jugemu 提示文本修正](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770878362773_hvqxev_HA3gUrLacAAqWGY.jpg)
![Lavart Agent Jugemu 提示文本修正](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770878363789_xjsooz_HA3gVT5akAAVZWr.jpg)

```
正しい表記に修正したテキストは以下の通りです:

「寿限無 寿限無 五劫の擦り切れ 海砂利水魚の 水行末 雲来末 風来末 食う寝る処に 住む処 藪ら柑子の 藪柑子 パイポ パイポ パイポの シューリンガン シューリンガンの グーリンダイ グーリンダイの ポンポコピーの ポンポコナーの 長久命の 長助」

それでは、このテキストが左上から右回転(時計回り)で渦を巻き、最後の文字「長助」が中心に来るデザインを生成いたします。
```

[[Lavart Agent Japanese Text Correction]]

### 44. 日文文本螺旋生成提示 (Jugemu)

**Author**: [ミサキ](https://x.com/misakin883)  **Date**: 2026-02-11  **Language**: ja

> 一个复杂的提示，旨在测试文本生成能力，要求将长篇日文故事《寿限无》的文本以顺时针螺旋形排列，从左上角开始，最终字符居中。此提示用于比较 Seedream 5.0 和 Nano Banana Pro。

![日文文本螺旋生成提示 (Jugemu)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770878362482_f3pgfr_HA3dmkcbEAAU2sB.jpg)
![日文文本螺旋生成提示 (Jugemu)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770878362659_1gww8p_HA3doWoboAEUGhl.jpg)

```
帯状になった以下の「」内の日本語の文字が左上から右回転で最後の文字が中心に来るように渦を巻いている。
「{argument name="テキスト" default="じゅげむ じゅげむ ごこうのすりきれ\n\nかいじゃりすいぎょの すいぎょうまつ うんらいまつ ふうらいまつ\n\nくうねるところに すむところ\n\nやぶらこうじの ぶらこうじ\n\nぱいぽ ぱいぽ ぱいぽの しゅーりんがん\n\nしゅーりんがんの ぐーりんだい\n\nぐーりんだいの ぽんぽこぴーの ぽんぽこなーの\n\nちょうきゅうめいの ちょうすけ"}」
文章は正しい日本語表記になるよう添削して修正してください。
```

[[Japanese Text Spiral Jugemu]]

### 61. 超写实高端时尚影棚男模肖像提示词（现代黑帮美学）

**Author**: [The Prompt Engineer](https://x.com/rorschachvibes)  **Date**: 2026-02-11  **Language**: en

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 模型提供一个详细的提示，以生成一张超现实、高级时装风格的影棚肖像，描绘一位自信的男性模特（25-30 岁），展现现代黑手党美学。该提示要求使用上传的参考图片，以 100% 准确地保留面部特征，并指定了炭灰色细条纹西装、深勃艮第色领带、后梳发型、可见的颈部和手指纹身，以及在深勃艮第色渐变背景下的电影级影棚灯光等细节。它强调极致的真实感和 8K 照片级质量。

[Jester bells clearly visible; costume stitching detail; blurred throne elements or stone arches as bokeh; shallow DOF falloff behind subject]

[Flash bloom halos on highlights; slight chromatic aberration on brightest edges; tiny compression grain; clean but tactile]

[Anachronistic contrast: High-gloss anime aesthetics vs. ancient medieval court texture; voyeuristic editorial energy (no UI/text); suggestive tension through pose and lighting]

- Cliffside dwellings embedded into rock faces, with arched openings, layered terraces, and organically curved facades.

- Sky-bridges and root-walkways connecting buildings, appearing load-bearing and structurally plausible.
- Transparent or semi-translucent roofing formed from bio-crystal membranes, allowing natural light into interiors.

No sharp industrial lines; all architecture follows structural logic and biological growth patterns.

[SUBSURFACE & STRUCTURAL CORE]

### 105. 切洋葱提示（文本/LLM）

**Author**: [보나](https://x.com/bbona_978)  **Date**: 2026-02-10  **Language**: ko

> “我没哭！”
> 
> “你哭了。”
> 
> “我才没哭！只是在切洋葱啦！”
> 
> “你手里根本没有洋葱。”
> 
> “……是我的心在切洋葱。”

```
“…왜 울었는데”
“………양파썰다가”
“왜 울었냐고”
“양파때문이라고 답했어”
“……내가 양파냐”

- 20260210 기특강쥐 프롬
```

**Author**: [Maercih](https://x.com/Maercihh)  **Date**: 2026-02-10  **Language**: en

> 一个极其详细、结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张在阳光充足的图书馆阁楼中女性的电影级写实肖像。它指定了相机设置（85mm，f1.8）、光线（黄金时段逆光）、构图和纹理质量，旨在达到高端编辑摄影的美学效果。

```
{
  "style": "cinematic realism, high-end editorial photography",
  "subject": {
    "type": "woman",
    "age_range": "mid-20s",
    "pose": "seated sideways on a bench, holding an open book, head turned slightly off-camera",
    "expression": "calm, reflective, distant gaze",
    "wardrobe": "deep black velvet wrap dress, soft texture, natural styling",
    "hair": "long, dark, loose waves, natural volume",
    "makeup": "minimal, realistic skin texture, no plastic smoothing"
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "sunlit library loft",
    "details": "tall glass windows, wooden shelves filled with books, warm interior tones, dust particles visible in air",
    "time_of_day": "golden hour",
    "atmosphere": "quiet, intimate, intellectual"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "strong golden hour backlight",
    "direction": "side-back window light",
    "effects": "natural lens flare, light streaks across frame, soft bloom on highlights, volumetric rays",
    "contrast": "medium-high with warm highlights and soft shadow falloff"
  },
  "camera": {
    "shot_type": "medium portrait",
    "angle": "slightly low eye-level",
    "lens": "85mm full-frame",
    "aperture": "f1.8",
    "depth_of_field": "shallow, subject sharp, background creamy blur",
    "focus": "eyes and face plane"
  },
  "color_grading": {
    "palette": "warm amber and honey tones with soft neutral shadows",
    "look": "film-like, subtle grain, cinematic dynamic range"
  },
  "composition": {
    "framing": "rule of thirds, subject right-weighted",
    "foreground": "soft blurred flare and book edge",
    "background": "window grid lines and shelves as leading lines",
    "motion": "still subject, drifting light particles"
  },
  "quality": {
    "resolution": "8k",
    "texture": "natural skin detail, realistic fabric texture",
    "rendering": "photorealistic, no over-sharpening, no CGI gloss"
  }
}

### 125. Z 世代青少年与 Q 版伙伴的混合媒体肖像

**Author**: [杉田 海地｜Saix CEO](https://x.com/SaixCEO)  **Date**: 2026-02-10  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个为 Gemini 的 Nano Banana Pro 设计的复杂多层提示，旨在创作一幅高质量的混合媒体肖像。主要主体是一位时尚的 Z 世代青少年（使用上传的照片），站在夜间火车站。图像将超现实主义摄影与彩色、扁平的卡通插图相结合，其中包含主体俏皮互动的“Q 版”形象。它包括对场景、服装的详细描述，以及叠加的手绘涂鸦效果，如标语和星星。

![Z 世代青少年与 Q 版伙伴的混合媒体肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770792216422_6cqzhn_HAx7B8EbAAAaxQu.jpg)

```
高品質なミックスメディアのポートレート。トレンディなZ世代のティーンエイジャー（私がアップロードした人物の写真を使用）が、夜の電車駅ホームに立っている。被写体はクールにポーズをとり、片手でオリーブ色のバックパックのストラップを持っている。  
服装はオシャレなZ世代スタイル（オーバーサイズのストリートウェア、レイヤードの黒いパーカー、グレーのスウェットパンツ、ゴツいスニーカー）。

背景にはリアルな「{argument name="train line" default="KRL Jabodetabek"}」コミューターラインの電車を横から見た姿が描かれ、特徴的な赤いストライプが入っている。電車のドアは大きく開いており、明るくシネマティックな駅の照明と都会の夜の雰囲気で照らされている。

リアルなメイン被写体の周りには、かわいい3D風の「ちび」バージョンが複数登場。同じ服装・同じ顔。  
ちびたちは遊び心たっぷりに絡んでいる：  
・1体は肩の上に座っている  
・1体は足に登っている  
・もう1体はバックパックから顔を覗かせている  

画像全体に鮮やかな手描きドゥードルエフェクトを重ねる：  
被写体を囲む白い手描きアウトライン、遊び心のある落書き、星、キラキラ、光のスパーク、  
そして浮遊する白と黒の手書きスローガン「{argument name="slogan 1" default="forever young"}」「krl」「night」「gen z vibes」など。  

スタイルはハイパーリアリスティックな写真と、カラフルでフラットなカートゥーンイラストがシームレスに融合したもの。  
顔と人物のシルエット・形は一切変更せず、そのまま保持。
```

[[Mixed Media Portrait]]

### 130. OOTD 贴纸风格解析

**Author**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0)  **Date**: 2026-02-10  **Language**: en

> 将上传的自拍照转换为风格化的“今日穿搭”（OOTD）图片，同时保持主体照片的真实感，并添加白色贴纸边框和美学时尚笔记本注释，模仿日韩时尚杂志的分解图。

![OOTD 贴纸风格解析](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770792206468_er6hyd_HAxsFcvacAANQJ9.jpg)

```
Mia OOTD Stickers Using my uploaded selfie as the exact reference, keep my face, body, proportions, and outfit completely unchanged with photorealistic accuracy.
Add white sticker-style borders around individual outfit items, as if they were cut out and pasted onto the image. Include aesthetic fashion notebook annotations, with soft pencil-style handwritten labels and arrows pointing to each item.
The annotations should feel like a scrapbook or fashion journal, minimal and clean, not overcrowded. Maintain the realism of the original photo while layering editorial-style outfit callouts on top.
Overall style feels like a Japanese/Korean fashion magazine OOTD breakdown, blending realistic photography with playful scrapbook elements, clean composition, soft tones, and a polished yet casual aesthetic.
```

### 132. UGC 风格时尚 Vlog 视频生成详细提示

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-02-10  **Language**: ja

> 一个与 Nano Banana Pro 和 Google Veo 3.1 配合使用的综合提示，用于生成一段视频片段，内容是一位女性以真实、温暖、亲密的 UGC（用户生成内容）风格的视频博客形式展示她的时尚。该提示详细说明了摄像机角度、灯光、主体表情、背景散景和对话。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、またはごく軽く手持ちし、被写体の真正面に配置（机や棚に置かれているように）。腕は既にフレーム外にある。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべており、まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

柔らかくボケた背景には[{argument name="背景設定" default="設定を追加する"}]が映っている。空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは[{argument name="ファッションの特徴" default="ファッションの特徴を追加"}]がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

### 139. 超现实黑白特写肖像，带发光线条

**Author**: [Harboriis](https://x.com/harboriis)  **Date**: 2026-02-10  **Language**: en

> 一个用于生成超逼真 8K 黑白微距肖像的提示。它着重于面部极致的特写细节，使用超现实的、波浪状的发光线条，像水下倒影一样在皮肤上荡漾，营造出一种私密而梦幻的美感。

![超现实黑白特写肖像，带发光线条](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770792189259_8ovbmo_HAw9-2TaAAYCFNU.jpg)
![超现实黑白特写肖像，带发光线条](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770792189354_o1imqi_HAw99RkaMAA-maz.jpg)

```
A hyperrealistic 8K black and white extreme close-up portrait of a young man's face, focusing tightly on his eye, cheekbone, and lips. Bright sunlight breaks into soft, wavy luminous lines that ripple across his skin like underwater reflections. The light flows diagonally, wrapping around the contours of his face in surreal patterns, while the shadows dissolve into smooth mid-gray tones instead of deep black. The skin is rendered in lifelike detail-visible pores, faint freckles, subtle stubble, and natural imperfections catch the glowing light realistically. The lips are softly highlighted, and the eye reflects fragments of the luminous waves, adding depth and emotion without artificial glow. The camera framing feels macro, pressed close to the face, with razor-thin depth of field: one illuminated ridge of skin is perfectly sharp, while the rest melts into velvety blur. The glassy, fluid quality of the light lines gives the portrait a surreal dreamlike aesthetic while remaining grounded in photographic realism. The background disappears into soft gray gradients, leaving only the interplay of skin texture and luminous wave-like rays. Fine cinematic grain overlays the frame, enhancing the tactile analog feel. The overall mood is intimate, surreal, and emotionally evocative - a monochrome portrait.
```

### 140. 时尚人像与中国龙旗袍

**Author**: [Aijaz](https://x.com/iamsofiaijaz)  **Date**: 2026-02-10  **Language**: en

> 生成一张引人注目的奢华时尚编辑肖像的提示语：一位优雅的女士，身穿带有精致红色龙纹刺绣的白色丝绸旗袍，手持一张带有火焰效果的红心皇后扑克牌，置身于戏剧性的中国龙浮雕背景前。

### 144. Nano Banana Pro 的提示技巧 (日文)

```
長めのテキストは入力を工夫する
　　┗単語や 分節の 合間に 半角スペースを入れて、こんなふうに 小学校1年生 の 教科書 みたいに 入力すると 出力結果が 良い

### 146. 高空抓拍：城市阶梯浪漫

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-02-09  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超逼真的偷拍照片，内容是一对情侣在欧洲城市楼梯上拥抱，从高处视角拍摄。它详细描述了环境（石头、砖石、复古栏杆）、服装、道具（男人背后藏着一束鲜花），并使用柔和的阴天日光来营造温暖、宁静、浪漫的氛围。

![高空抓拍：城市阶梯浪漫](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770706156788_fxjbzz_HAv4P_TaAAcBsNi.jpg)
![高空抓拍：城市阶梯浪漫](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770706156873_tgbyxg_HAv4P_UaAAMMIIg.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "task_type": "photoreal_candid_city_stairs_romance",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v1.0_OVERHEAD_STAIRS_HUG_FLOWERS_BEHIND_BACK"
    },
    "output": {
      "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
      "resolution": "high",
      "num_images": 4
    },
    "scene": {
      "concept": "a quiet romantic moment captured from above on a city staircase",
      "environment": "stone staircase with red-brown masonry wall, vintage iron railing, European urban setting, clean background with architectural texture",
      "composition": "elevated viewpoint looking down, couple centered on the stairs, railing partially in foreground for depth, strong leading lines from steps"
    },
    "subject": {
      "couple": "adult woman and adult man",
      "wardrobe": {
        "woman": "{argument name="woman's coat" default="beige trench coat"}, long dark hair, carrying a light neutral handbag",
        "man": "short-sleeve light shirt under a brown knit sweater vest, dark trousers"
      },
      "prop": "bouquet of {argument name="flower color" default="bright pink"} flowers wrapped in paper, held behind man’s back",
      "pose": "close hug, woman’s arms around his shoulders, calm intimate expression",
      "emotion": "soft, romantic, private moment"
    },
    "camera": {
      "shot": "telephoto candid from elevated angle",
      "lens_mm": 85,
      "aperture": 2.8,
      "focus": "sharp on couple and bouquet; background architecture slightly softened",
      "quality_tags": "ultra-photoreal, crisp textures, natural skin detail"
    },
    "lighting": {
      "style": "soft overcast daylight",
      "notes": "no flash, balanced exposure, preserve stone texture and bouquet color without oversaturation"
    },
    "color_grade": {
      "palette": "muted neutrals brown with a pop of pink flowers",
      "contrast": "gentle documentary contrast",
      "tone": "warm, quiet, romantic"
    },
    "negative_prompt": "text, logo, watermark, blur, lowres, deformed hands, extra fingers, warped stairs, crooked railing, CGI, cartoon, harsh flash, oversaturated colors, heavy artifacts"
  }
}
```

**Author**: [Lloyd Creates](https://x.com/lloydcreates)  **Date**: 2026-02-09  **Language**: en

> 一个高度技术化、结构化的提示，用于生成产品可视化，采用“流体镀铬扭曲”效果，产品在纯黑色的虚空背景下，溶解成光滑、流动的虹彩蓝银液态金属垂直条纹，强调柔和的渐变和无硬边。

![流体 Chrome 扭曲产品渲染](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770706179087_rds2wr_HAuXaHaXoAApqk-.jpg)

```
{
  "product_type": "{argument name=\"product type\" default=\"[PRODUCT]\"}",
  "prompt": "A [product_type] floating against a pure black void background (#000000). The product is small and centered in frame with generous black negative space on all sides, the product occupies no more than 50% of the frame and is never cropped. The product is visualized through a liquid vertical streak effect, as if the product has been melted and stretched into smooth, flowing vertical streaks of liquid metal. The streaks are buttery smooth, fluid, and organic like mercury or molten silver flowing downward. Each streak blends and bleeds softly into the next with no hard edges, no sharp block corners, no rigid geometry. The vertical streaks have varying thickness and luminosity, creating a sense of depth and dimensionality. The liquid streaks glow with cool monochromatic {argument name=\"color tone\" default=\"blue-silver\"} iridescent tones, think liquid mercury under blue light. The streaks flow smoothly with gentle luminous gradients, bright specular highlights fading into deep shadow. The effect is contained within the product's general silhouette shape with pure black void surrounding it. The overall impression should be a product dissolving into smooth vertical streams of liquid light. No hard edges, no blocky slats, no rigid bars.",
  "negative_prompt": "hard edges, sharp corners, blocky slats, rigid bars, chrome blocks, machined metal, solid geometric shapes, cropped product, cut off edges, radial pattern, circular rings, horizontal lines, warm colors, red, orange, yellow, green, colored background, flat lighting, matte surface",
  "style_parameters": {
    "background_color": "#000000 pure black void",
    "effect": "smooth liquid vertical streaks, fluid mercury-like, buttery soft, no hard edges",
    "effect_color": "iridescent monochromatic liquid blue-silver #C0C0C0",
    "pattern_type": "flowing liquid metal vertical streaks with soft gradients — NOT rigid blocks or bars",
    "product_framing": "centered, small in frame, max 50% canvas, NEVER cropped, generous black space",
    "product_color": "liquid mercury blue-silver iridescent",
    "lighting": "smooth luminous gradients, soft specular highlights, liquid light quality"
  }
}
```

![AI 辅助小说创作与封面生成工作流](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770706244312_2ionu8_HAuE3LzaoAAPtD3.jpg)

![AI 辅助小说创作与封面生成工作流](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770706245751_24qkwa_HAuE3LvakAAIQ5L.jpg)

```
好みの画像を一枚参考にさせて

・画像を小説の表紙に見立ててタイトルを考えて
⬇
・表紙とタイトルから内容のあらすじとチャプターを総字数{argument name="総字数" default="○○字"}想定で考案して
⬇
各チャプターを順に執筆して
```

```
カラスアゲハ春型♂、展翅標本の表裏比較。左の構造色と右の{argument name="色" default="matte褐色"}が同じ蝶だということがこの図版の情報量。AIに「iridescent」と書くと全部光る。「ここだけ光る、ここは光らない」を書き分けるのがプロンプトの仕事。
```

### 183. 详细电影武侠场景提示：暗鸦 对战 碧霜

**Author**: [李岳](https://x.com/liyue_ai)  **Date**: 2026-02-09  **Language**: zh

> 一个极其详细、多场景的提示，专为电影级视频或图像生成设计，侧重于武侠（中国武术奇幻）风格。它概述了五个不同的镜头，角色动作，视觉元素（瓢泼大雨、古老寺庙、闪电），摄像机运动（推轨镜头、升降镜头、子弹时间），对话，以及音效，旨在呈现“暗鸦”与“碧霜”两位角色之间戏剧性的对决。

![详细电影武侠场景提示：暗鸦 对战 碧霜](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770706236748_k3nyz6_HArlGrtaIAEz-bU.jpg)
![详细电影武侠场景提示：暗鸦 对战 碧霜](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770706236742_vjdtu2_HArlGrybAAE558O.jpg)

```
整体风格提示： 中国武侠玄幻风格，电影质感，动态模糊，暴雨中的废弃古寺，阴郁的天空，闪电不时照亮雨滴和残破的飞檐，画面充满力量与速度感。

• 镜头1 (0-3秒)：暗鸦拖剑，青霜降临 
• 画面：暴雨如注。暗鸦身披散发不祥紫气的黑色重铠，单手拖着一把缠绕锁链的玄铁巨剑，剑刃在石板地上划出刺目的火星与波纹。他眼神阴鸷，看向前方。紧接着，青霜从古寺残破的屋檐上如一片落叶般轻盈飘落，白青相间的劲装飒爽，高马尾飞扬，手中青色长剑“锃”然出鞘，寒气逼开周身雨幕。两人在雨中对峙。 
• 运镜：极低角度跟拍巨剑划地的轨迹，随后镜头快速拉远，展现暴雨庭院中一黑一青、一沉重一轻灵的对峙全景。 
• 对话/音效：暗鸦（低沉沙哑）：“{argument name="暗鸦台詞" default="执迷不悟。"}” 
• 音效：沉重的金属摩擦声、滂沱雨声、风声。 

• 镜头2 (3-6秒)：重剑横扫，轻剑惊鸿 • 画面：暗鸦猛然发力，双臂挥动巨剑，一道半月形的黑色剑气撕裂雨幕横扫而出，所过之处雨滴蒸发，地面石板被犁开。青霜眼神一凝，脚尖轻点水面，身形如鹞子般冲天而起，在空中一个灵巧的侧翻，惊险地避开剑气。同时，她借下坠之势，剑尖寒光凝聚，如流星般直刺暗鸦咽喉。 
• 运镜：快节奏切镜。先是一个侧面跟拍（Dolly Shot）捕捉黑色剑气切碎无数雨滴的慢动作瞬间，旋即切换至仰拍视角，展现青霜空中闪避与反击的优美轨迹。
• 音效：巨剑破空的沉重呼啸、剑气蒸发的“嗤嗤”声、衣袂破风声。 

• 镜头3 (6-9秒)：空中对撼，火花迸射 • 画面：暗鸦巨剑回撩，与青霜下刺的长剑精准对撞！“铛——！”巨剑的磅礴力量与长剑的灵巧寒气激烈对抗，爆发出耀眼的蓝白色火花与一圈震荡波，将周围雨水全部震开。暗鸦凭借力量优势向下压制，青霜则施展轻功，足尖在巨剑上一点，借力向后空翻，化解千斤重压。 
• 运镜：环绕运镜（Bullet Time）。镜头以两人武器碰撞点为中心，进行360度快速旋转，最后定格在火花最璀璨、两人力量抗衡的瞬间特写。 
• 对话/音效：青霜（清冷坚定）：“{argument name="青霜台詞" default="邪不胜正！"}” 
• 音效：巨大的金属撞击轰鸣、力量对抗的嗡嗡声。 

• 镜头4 (9-12秒)：青影连绵，黑壁固守 
• 画面：落地瞬间，青霜率先发动攻势。她身形化为一道青色残影，手中长剑疾刺，瞬间化为数道凌厉的青色剑光，从不同角度刺向暗鸦，剑尖寒气在空中留下道道霜痕。暗鸦低吼一声，将沉重的巨剑舞得密不透风，形成一面紫黑色的剑气屏障。密集的“叮当”声中，青色剑光尽数被挡下，但强大的冲击力仍逼得暗鸦“蹬蹬蹬”后退三步，每一步都将脚下的石砖踩得粉碎。 
• 运镜：一镜到底的手持跟拍（Shaky Cam）。镜头紧贴青霜的进攻轨迹移动，伴随每一次刺击产生轻微抖动，随后迅速摇到暗鸦的防守和后退，代入感极强。 
• 音效：剑尖撞击屏障的密集清脆声响、石砖碎裂声、沉重的脚步声与喘息。 

• 镜头5 (12-15秒)：终极碰撞，气吞寰宇 
• 画面：暗鸦暴怒，将全身紫气注入巨剑，猛地插入地面！轰隆！一道粗大的紫黑色光柱冲天而起，搅动天上乌云。青霜毫无惧色，将全部寒气灌注剑身，人剑合一，化为一道巨大、纯粹的青色流光，如彗星般从天而降，直刺光柱中心。两者轰然对撞！时间仿佛静止，随即爆发吞没一切的刺眼白光与环形气浪，将整个庭院的雨水、瓦砾、枯叶全部向外排空。 
• 运镜：特写急速拉升。先是暗鸦阴冷双眼和青霜坚毅眼眸的快速对切特写，随后镜头如火箭般急速向后上方拉升（Crane Up），变成俯瞰远景，展现爆炸白光膨胀、气浪席卷古寺废墟的震撼全景。画面在白光最盛处定格。 
• 对话/音效：（碰撞前）暗鸦的怒吼与青霜的清吒交织。
• 音效：能量汇聚的嗡鸣、震撼天地的爆炸声、随后一切声音收束，只余雨声渐弱的回响。
```

[[Wuxia Battle Scene]]
